\DoxyCodeLine{158 }
\DoxyCodeLine{159   \textcolor{comment}{// We probe the hash table in groups of |kGroupWidth| buckets. One bucket}}
\DoxyCodeLine{160   \textcolor{comment}{// corresponds to a 1-\/byte entry in the control table.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{161   \textcolor{comment}{// Each group can be uniquely identified by the index of its first bucket,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{162   \textcolor{comment}{// which must be a value between 0 (inclusive) and Capacity() (exclusive).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{163   \textcolor{comment}{// Note that logically, groups wrap around after index Capacity() -\/ 1. This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{164   \textcolor{comment}{// means that probing the group starting at, for example, index Capacity() -\/ 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{165   \textcolor{comment}{// means probing CtrlTable()[Capacity() -\/ 1] followed by CtrlTable()[0] to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{166   \textcolor{comment}{// CtrlTable()[6], assuming a group width of 8. However, in memory, this is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{167   \textcolor{comment}{// achieved by maintaining an additional |kGroupWidth| bytes after the first}}
\DoxyCodeLine{168   \textcolor{comment}{// Capacity() entries of the control table. These contain a copy of the first}}
\DoxyCodeLine{169   \textcolor{comment}{// max(Capacity(), kGroupWidth) entries of the control table. If Capacity() <}}
\DoxyCodeLine{170   \textcolor{comment}{// |kGroupWidth|, then the remaining |kGroupWidth| -\/ Capacity() control bytes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{171   \textcolor{comment}{// are left as |kEmpty|.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{172   \textcolor{comment}{// This means that actually, probing the group starting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{173   \textcolor{comment}{// at index Capacity() -\/ 1 is achieved by probing CtrlTable()[Capacity() -\/ 1],}}
\DoxyCodeLine{174   \textcolor{comment}{// followed by CtrlTable()[Capacity()] to CtrlTable()[Capacity() + 7].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{175 }
\DoxyCodeLine{176   \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1internal_1_1SwissNameDictionary_aeacd57fe405f3ea6b386c35657fc8c31}{ctrl\_t}}* ctrl = \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1internal_1_1SwissNameDictionary_af39315384fcdb116923e08f7948e99e1}{CtrlTable}}();}

\DoxyCodeLine{191 }
\DoxyCodeLine{192     \textcolor{comment}{// The following selects the next group to probe. Note that seq.offset()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{193     \textcolor{comment}{// always advances by a multiple of |kGroupWidth|, modulo Capacity(). This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{194     \textcolor{comment}{// is done in a way such that we visit Capacity() / |kGroupWidth|}}

\DoxyCodeLine{199     \textcolor{comment}{// If the following DCHECK weren't true, we would have probed all Capacity()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{200     \textcolor{comment}{// different buckets without finding one containing |kEmpty| (which would}}
\DoxyCodeLine{201     \textcolor{comment}{// haved triggered the g.MatchEmpty() check above). This must not be the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{202     \textcolor{comment}{// case because the maximum load factor of 7/8 guarantees that there must}}
\DoxyCodeLine{203     \textcolor{comment}{// always remain empty buckets.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{204     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{205     \textcolor{comment}{// The only exception from this rule are small tables, where 2 * Capacity()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{206     \textcolor{comment}{// < |kGroupWidth|, in which case all Capacity() entries can be filled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{207     \textcolor{comment}{// without leaving empty buckets. The layout of the control}}
\DoxyCodeLine{208     \textcolor{comment}{// table guarantees that after the first Capacity() entries of the control}}
\DoxyCodeLine{209     \textcolor{comment}{// table, the control table contains a copy of those first Capacity()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{210     \textcolor{comment}{// entries, followed by kGroupWidth -\/ 2 * Capacity() entries containing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{211     \textcolor{comment}{// |kEmpty|. This guarantees that the g.MatchEmpty() check above will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{212     \textcolor{comment}{// always trigger if the element wasn't found, correctly preventing us from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{213     \textcolor{comment}{// probing more than one group in this special case.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{371 }
\DoxyCodeLine{372   \textcolor{comment}{// The ctrl table contains a copy of the first group (i.e., the group starting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{373   \textcolor{comment}{// at entry 0) after the first |capacity| entries of the ctrl table. This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{374   \textcolor{comment}{// means that the ctrl table always has size |capacity| + |kGroupWidth|.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{375   \textcolor{comment}{// However, note that we may have |capacity| < |kGroupWidth|. For example, if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{376   \textcolor{comment}{// Capacity() == 8 and |kGroupWidth| == 16, then ctrl[0] is copied to ctrl[8],}}
\DoxyCodeLine{377   \textcolor{comment}{// ctrl[1] to ctrl[9], etc. In this case, ctrl[16] to ctrl[23] remain unused,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{378   \textcolor{comment}{// which means that their values are always Ctrl::kEmpty.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{379   \textcolor{comment}{// We achieve the necessary copying without branching here using some bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{380   \textcolor{comment}{// magic: We set \{copy\_entry = entry\} in those cases where we don't actually}}
\DoxyCodeLine{381   \textcolor{comment}{// have to perform a copy (meaning that we just repeat the \{ctrl[entry] = h\}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{382   \textcolor{comment}{// from above). If we do need to do some actual copying, we set \{copy\_entry =}}
\DoxyCodeLine{383   \textcolor{comment}{// Capacity() + entry\}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{384 }
\DoxyCodeLine{385   \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} mask = capacity -\/ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{386   \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} copy\_entry =}
\DoxyCodeLine{387       ((\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1internal_1_1SwissNameDictionary_a2739932dc23ef6afc20447e03be06f6a}{entry}} -\/ \mbox{\hyperlink{structv8_1_1internal_1_1swiss__table_1_1GroupPortableImpl_a85906a0176ab7d8fcda4ec3851fe05a6}{Group::kWidth}}) \& mask) + 1 + ((\mbox{\hyperlink{structv8_1_1internal_1_1swiss__table_1_1GroupPortableImpl_a85906a0176ab7d8fcda4ec3851fe05a6}{Group::kWidth}} -\/ 1) \& mask);}
